        <script type="text/javascript">
            function ShowForm(e) {
                let SearchBlock = document.getElementsByClassName("search-block")[0];
                if (SearchBlock.classList.contains("d-flex")) {
                    document.getElementsByClassName("search-block")[0].classList.remove("d-flex");
                    document.getElementsByClassName("search-block")[0].classList.add("d-none");
                } else {
                    document.getElementsByClassName("search-block")[0].classList.add("d-flex");
                    document.getElementsByClassName("search-block")[0].classList.remove("d-none");
                }
            }
        </script>

            <script>
                document.getElementById("search-submit").addEventListener("click", async function(event) {
                    event.preventDefault();
                    let search = document.getElementById("search");
                    search.value = search.value.trim();
                    search.value = search.value.replace("://dl.flipkart.com/dlhttp://", "://");
                    search.value = search.value.replace("://dl.flipkart.com/dlhttps://", "://");
                    search.value = search.value.replace(/http:\/\//g, " http://");
                    search.value = search.value.replace(/https:\/\//g, " https://");
                    search.value = search.value.replace(/https:\/\/dl.flipkart.com/g, " http://dl.flipkart.com");
                    search.value = search.value.replace("//m.flipkart.com/", "//www.flipkart.com/");
                    search.value = search.value.replace("dl.flipkart.com/dl/", " www.flipkart.com/");
                    if (search.value.length == 0) {
                        document.getElementById("search-message").getElementsByTagName("div")[0].innerText = "Please search something!";
                        document.getElementById("search-message").classList.remove("d-none");
                        return;
                    }
                    while (search.value.length > 1 && search.value[search.value.length - 1] == "=") {
                        search.value = search.value.slice(0, -1);
                    }
                    const matches = search.value.match(/\bhttps?:\/\/\S+/gi);
                    if (matches != null && matches.length > 0) {
                        try {
                            let domain = new URL(matches[0]).hostname;
                            if (domain.toLowerCase().includes("amazon.com")) {
                                window.location.href = "https://pricehistory.app/page/search#gsc.tab=0&gsc.q=" + encodeURIComponent(search.value);
                                return
                            }
                        } catch (error) {}
                        document.getElementsByClassName("loader-container")[0].classList.remove("d-none");
                        fetch("https://pricehistory.app/" + "api/search", {
                            method: 'POST',
                            headers: {
                                'Content-Type': 'application/json',
                            },
                            body: JSON.stringify({
                                url: matches[0]
                            }),
                        }).then( (response) => response.json()).then( (data) => {
                            if (data.status) {
                                window.location.href = "https://pricehistory.app/p\/" + data.code;
                            } else {
                                document.getElementById("search-message").getElementsByTagName("div")[0].innerText = data.message;
                                document.getElementById("search-message").classList.remove("d-none");
                                document.getElementsByClassName("loader-container")[0].classList.add("d-none");
                            }
                        }
                        ).catch( (error) => {
                            console.error('Error:', error);
                            document.getElementById("search-message").getElementsByTagName("div")[0].innerText = "Sorry,Something went wrong!";
                            document.getElementById("search-message").classList.remove("d-none");
                            document.getElementsByClassName("loader-container")[0].classList.add("d-none");
                        }
                        );
                    } else {
                        window.location.href = "https://pricehistory.app/page/search#gsc.tab=0&gsc.q=" + encodeURIComponent(search.value);
                    }
                });
                document.getElementById("search-message").getElementsByTagName("span")[0].addEventListener("click", function(e) {
                    document.getElementById("search-message").classList.add("d-none");
                });
                let queryString = window.location.search.replace(/\+\&/g, "+").replace(/\+\=/g, "+").replace(/\+\&/g, "+").replace(/\+\=/g, "+");
                const searchParams = {};
                if (queryString) {
                    queryString.substr(1).split('&').forEach(param => {
                        const [key,value] = param.split('=');
                        if (value && value.length > 0) {
                            try {
                                searchParams[key] = decodeURIComponent(value.replace(/\+/g, '%20'));
                            } catch (error) {
                                searchParams[key] = "" + (value.replace(/\+/g, ' '));
                            }
                        } else {
                            searchParams['search'] += key.replace(/\+/g, ' ');
                        }
                    }
                    );
                }
                if (searchParams['search'] != undefined) {
                    document.getElementById("search").value = searchParams['search'];
                    setTimeout( () => {
                        document.getElementById("search-submit").click();
                    }
                    , 500)
                }
            </script>
            <script>
                function ShareIntent(Title, Message) {
                    try {
                        PriceHistoryApp.shareTextUrl(Title, Message);
                    } catch (e) {
                        if (navigator.share) {
                            navigator.share({
                                title: Title,
                                text: Message,
                            }).then( () => console.log('Successful share')).catch( (error) => console.log('Error sharing', error));
                        } else {
                            const el = document.createElement('textarea');
                            el.value = Message;
                            document.body.appendChild(el);
                            el.select();
                            document.execCommand('copy');
                            document.body.removeChild(el);
                            DisplayMessage("Copied <br> <small>Now you can share it anywhere!</small>");
                        }
                    }
                }
                function CopyUrl() {
                    const el = document.createElement('textarea');
                    el.value = window.location.href;
                    document.body.appendChild(el);
                    el.select();
                    document.execCommand('copy');
                    document.body.removeChild(el);
                    DisplayMessage("URL Copied <br> <small>Now you can share URL to anywhere!</small>");
                }
                var DisplayMessageClickTracker = true;
                function DisplayMessage(msg="Thank You") {
                    document.getElementById("displaymessage-text").innerHTML = msg;
                    if (DisplayMessageClickTracker && document.querySelector("#displaymessage").classList.contains('d-none')) {
                        DisplayMessageClickTracker = false;
                        document.querySelector("#displaymessage").classList.remove('d-none');
                        setTimeout( () => {
                            DisplayMessageClickTracker = true;
                            document.querySelector("#displaymessage").classList.add('d-none');
                        }
                        , 1050)
                    }
                }
                document.getElementById("phse-modal").getElementsByClassName("close")[0].addEventListener("click", (e) => {
                    document.getElementById("phse-modal").getElementsByTagName("iframe")[0].remove();
                    document.getElementById("phse-modal").style.display = "none";
                }
                );
                function ShowSearchResult(Code, Name) {
                    try {
                        document.getElementById("phse-modal").getElementsByTagName("iframe")[0].remove();
                    } catch (error) {}
                    let iframe = document.createElement("iframe");
                    iframe.src = `https://pricehistory.app/searchexperiance/${Code}#gsc.tab=0&gsc.q=${Name}`;
                    iframe.frameBorder = 0;
                    document.getElementById("phse-modal").getElementsByClassName("modal-content")[0].append(iframe);
                    document.getElementById("phse-modal").style.display = "block";
                }
            </script>

    if (false && window.location.host == "pricehistory.app") {

<script>
    document.addEventListener("DOMContentLoaded", function() {
        let PriceDropShowLimit = 6;
        var showAllBtn = document.getElementById("show-all-drops-btn");
        var showRecentBtn = document.getElementById("show-recent-drops-btn");
        var items = document.querySelectorAll(".price-drop-item");
        showAllBtn.addEventListener("click", function() {
            items.forEach(function(item) {
                item.classList.remove("d-none");
            });
            showAllBtn.classList.add("d-none");
            showRecentBtn.classList.remove("d-none");
        });
        showRecentBtn.addEventListener("click", function() {
            items.forEach(function(item, idx) {
                if (idx < PriceDropShowLimit) {
                    item.classList.remove("d-none");
                } else {
                    item.classList.add("d-none");
                }
            });
            showAllBtn.classList.remove("d-none");
            showRecentBtn.classList.add("d-none");
        });
    });
</script>

    function UpdateEnabled() {
        let d = new Date();
        d.setFullYear(d.getFullYear() - 1);
        EnabledLimits.Year = (d.getTime() > EnabledLimits.MinStamp) ? true : false;
        d = new Date();
        d.setMonth(d.getMonth() - 6);
        EnabledLimits.SixMonth = (d.getTime() > EnabledLimits.MinStamp) ? true : false;
        d = new Date();
        d.setMonth(d.getMonth() - 3);
        EnabledLimits.ThreeMonth = (d.getTime() > EnabledLimits.MinStamp) ? true : false;
        d = new Date();
        d.setMonth(d.getMonth() - 1);
        EnabledLimits.Month = (d.getTime() > EnabledLimits.MinStamp) ? true : false;
        if (EnabledLimits.Year != null && EnabledLimits.Year) {
            document.getElementById("chart-action-button-1y").classList.remove("d-none");
        }
        if (EnabledLimits.SixMonth != null && EnabledLimits.SixMonth) {
            document.getElementById("chart-action-button-6m").classList.remove("d-none");
        }
        if (EnabledLimits.ThreeMonth != null && EnabledLimits.ThreeMonth) {
            document.getElementById("chart-action-button-3m").classList.remove("d-none");
        }
        if (EnabledLimits.Month != null && EnabledLimits.Month) {
            document.getElementById("chart-action-button-1m").classList.remove("d-none");
        }
        document.getElementById("chart-action-button-reset").classList.remove("d-none");
        document.getElementById("chart-action-button-all").classList.remove("d-none");
        if (document.getElementById('PriceHistoryChart').classList.contains("animation")) {
            document.getElementById('PriceHistoryChart').classList.remove("animation");
        }
    }
    function UpdateChartZoom(mode) {
        let d = new Date();
        chart.options.scales.x.max = d.getTime();
        switch (mode) {
        case "left":
            chart.pan({
                x: (chart.getZoomLevel("y") * EnabledLimits.PanLeft)
            });
            return;
            break;
        case "right":
            chart.pan({
                x: (chart.getZoomLevel("y") * EnabledLimits.PanRight)
            });
            return;
            break;
        case "in":
            chart.zoom({
                x: EnabledLimits.ZoomIn
            });
            break;
        case "out":
            chart.zoom({
                x: EnabledLimits.ZoomOut
            });
            break;
        case "1y":
            d.setFullYear(d.getFullYear() - 1);
            chart.options.scales.x.min = d.getTime();
            break;
        case "6m":
            d.setMonth(d.getMonth() - 6);
            chart.options.scales.x.min = d.getTime();
            break;
        case "3m":
            d.setMonth(d.getMonth() - 3);
            chart.options.scales.x.min = d.getTime();
            break;
        case "1m":
            d.setMonth(d.getMonth() - 2);
            chart.options.scales.x.min = d.getTime();
            break;
        case "all":
            chart.options.scales.x.min = EnabledLimits.MinStamp;
            break;
        default:
            UpdateChartZoom("all");
            return;
            if (EnabledLimits.SixMonth == true) {
                UpdateChartZoom("6m");
            } else if (EnabledLimits.ThreeMonth == true) {
                UpdateChartZoom("3m");
            } else if (EnabledLimits.Year == true) {
                UpdateChartZoom("1y");
            } else if (EnabledLimits.Month == true) {
                UpdateChartZoom("1m");
            } else {
                UpdateChartZoom("all");
            }
            return;
            break;
        }
        chart.update();
    }
    const TooltipText = (tooltipItems) => {
        if (tooltipItems.datasetIndex == 0) {
            return "Offer Price:‚Çπ" + tooltipItems.parsed.y;
        } else if (tooltipItems.datasetIndex == 1) {
            return "Price:‚Çπ" + tooltipItems.parsed.y;
        } else {
            return "Price:‚Çπ" + tooltipItems.parsed.y;
        }
    }
    ;
    const TooltipFooter = (tooltipFooter) => {
        try {
            let FooterText = "";
            let AllAnotations = tooltipFooter[0].chart.config._config.options.plugins.annotation.annotations;
            for (let i = 0; i < AllAnotations.length; i++) {
                if (AllAnotations[i].type == "box" && new Date(tooltipFooter[0].raw.x) >= new Date(AllAnotations[i].xMin) && new Date(tooltipFooter[0].raw.x) <= new Date(AllAnotations[i].xMax) && "label"in AllAnotations[i] && "content"in AllAnotations[i].label && AllAnotations[i].label.content.length > 1) {
                    return AllAnotations[i].label.content;
                }
            }
            return "";
        } catch (error) {
            return "";
        }
    }
    ;
    const TooltipTitle = (tooltipItems) => {
        let d = new Date(tooltipItems[0].parsed.x);
        return d.toLocaleDateString('en-IN', {
            day: 'numeric',
            month: 'long',
            year: 'numeric',
        })
    }

                    rangeMax: {

                display: false,

    ;function UpdatePrices(Prices) {
        let flag = false;
        if ("History"in Prices) {
            let ChartDataSets = [];
            if ("Price"in Prices.History && Prices.History.Price != null && Array.isArray(Prices.History.Price) && Prices.History.Price.length > 0) {
                if ("OfferPrice"in Prices.History && Prices.History.OfferPrice != null && Array.isArray(Prices.History.OfferPrice) && Prices.History.OfferPrice.length > 0) {
                    ChartDataSets.push({
                        type: "scatter",
                        label: "Offer Price",
                        data: Prices.History.OfferPrice,
                        backgroundColor: '#ff534b',
                        borderColor: '#ff534b',
                        pointRadius: 3,
                    });
                }
                if (Prices.History.Price.length == 1) {
                    ChartDataSets.push({
                        type: "line",
                        label: "Prices",
                        data: Prices.History.Price,
                        borderJoinStyle: "round",
                        pointRadius: 2,
                        borderWidth: 1,
                        backgroundColor: '#FFFFFFFF',
                        borderColor: '#17a2b8',
                    });
                } else {
                    ChartDataSets.push({
                        type: "line",
                        label: "Prices",
                        data: Prices.History.Price,
                        borderJoinStyle: "round",
                        pointRadius: 0,
                        fill: true,
                        borderWidth: 2,
                        backgroundColor: '#17a2b833',
                        borderColor: '#17a2b8',
                    });
                }
                flag = true;
            }
            if (flag == true && ChartDataSets.length > 0) {
                let start_date = new Date(Prices.History.Price[0].x);
                let end_date = new Date(Prices.History.Price[Prices.History.Price.length - 1].x);
                let range_min = new Date(Prices.History.Price[0].x);
                let range_max = new Date(Prices.History.Price[Prices.History.Price.length - 1].x);
                ChartOptions.scales.x.min = start_date.toDateString();
                ChartOptions.scales.x.max = end_date.toDateString();
                EnabledLimits.MaxStamp = end_date.getTime();
                EnabledLimits.MinStamp = start_date.getTime();
                ChartOptions.plugins.zoom.pan.rangeMin.x = range_min;
                ChartOptions.plugins.zoom.zoom.rangeMin.x = range_min;
                ChartOptions.plugins.zoom.limits.x.min = range_min;
                ChartOptions.plugins.zoom.pan.rangeMax.x = range_max;
                ChartOptions.plugins.zoom.zoom.rangeMax.x = range_max;
                ChartOptions.plugins.zoom.limits.x.max = range_max;
                if ("Price"in Prices && "MinPrice"in Prices.Price && Prices.Price.MinPrice && Prices.Price.MinPrice != null) {
                    ChartOptions.plugins.zoom.pan.rangeMin.y = parseInt(Prices.Price.MinPrice - ((Prices.Price.MinPrice * 10) / 100));
                    ChartOptions.plugins.zoom.zoom.rangeMin.y = parseInt(Prices.Price.MinPrice - ((Prices.Price.MinPrice * 10) / 100));
                    ChartOptions.plugins.zoom.limits.y.min = parseInt(Prices.Price.MinPrice - ((Prices.Price.MinPrice * 10) / 100));
                }
                if ("Price"in Prices && "MaxPrice"in Prices.Price && Prices.Price.MaxPrice && Prices.Price.MaxPrice != null) {
                    let TempData = 0;
                    if ("TotalPrice"in Prices.Price && Prices.Price.TotalPrice && Prices.Price.TotalPrice != null && "Count"in Prices.Price && Prices.Price.Count && Prices.Price.Count != null && "MinPrice"in Prices.Price && Prices.Price.MinPrice && Prices.Price.MinPrice != null) {
                        TempData = parseInt(Prices.Price.MaxPrice + (((((Prices.Price.MaxPrice - (Prices.Price.TotalPrice / Prices.Price.Count)) * 5) / 100) + (((Prices.Price.MaxPrice - Prices.Price.MinPrice) * 5) / 100)) / 2));
                    }
                    if (TempData > 0) {
                        ChartOptions.plugins.zoom.pan.rangeMax.y = TempData;
                        ChartOptions.plugins.zoom.zoom.rangeMax.y = TempData;
                        ChartOptions.plugins.zoom.limits.y.max = TempData;
                        ChartOptions.scales.y.max = TempData;
                    } else {
                        ChartOptions.plugins.zoom.pan.rangeMax.y = parseInt(Prices.Price.MaxPrice + ((Prices.Price.MaxPrice * 10) / 100));
                        ChartOptions.plugins.zoom.zoom.rangeMax.y = parseInt(Prices.Price.MaxPrice + ((Prices.Price.MaxPrice * 10) / 100));
                        ChartOptions.plugins.zoom.limits.y.max = parseInt(Prices.Price.MaxPrice + ((Prices.Price.MaxPrice * 10) / 100));
                        ChartOptions.scales.y.max = parseInt(Prices.Price.MaxPrice + ((Prices.Price.MaxPrice * 5) / 100));
                    }
                }
                if ("Price"in Prices && "Count"in Prices.Price && Prices.Price.Count != null && typeof Prices.Price.Count == "number" && Prices.Price.Count > 1) {
                    ChartOptions.plugins.annotation = {
                        annotations: []
                    };
                    let PriceAnotationStarts = {
                        Lowest: null,
                        Highest: null,
                        LowestOffer: null,
                        Total: 0,
                        Count: 0
                    };
                    if (!("MaxPrice"in Prices.Price && Prices.Price.MaxPrice && Prices.Price.MaxPrice != null && "MinPrice"in Prices.Price && Prices.Price.MinPrice && Prices.Price.MinPrice != null && Prices.Price.MinPrice == Prices.Price.MaxPrice)) {
                        if ("MinPrice"in Prices.Price && Prices.Price.MinPrice && Prices.Price.MinPrice != null) {
                            ChartOptions.plugins.annotation.annotations.push({
                                type: 'line',
                                mode: 'horizontal',
                                scaleID: 'y',
                                value: Prices.Price.MinPrice,
                                borderColor: '#17a2b899',
                                borderWidth: 1,
                                label: {
                                    backgroundColor: '#17a2b8bb',
                                    drawTime: 'afterDatasetsDraw',
                                    content: 'Lowest:‚Çπ' + Prices.Price.MinPrice,
                                    enabled: true,
                                    position: "start",
                                    font: {
                                        size: 10
                                    },
                                    padding: 3,
                                    display: true
                                }
                            });
                            if ("MinOfferPrice"in Prices.Price && Prices.Price.MinOfferPrice && Prices.Price.MinOfferPrice != null && Prices.Price.MinOfferPrice < Prices.Price.MinPrice) {
                                ChartOptions.plugins.annotation.annotations.push({
                                    type: 'line',
                                    mode: 'horizontal',
                                    scaleID: 'y',
                                    value: Prices.Price.MinOfferPrice,
                                    borderColor: '#28a74599',
                                    borderWidth: 1,
                                    label: {
                                        backgroundColor: '#28a745bb',
                                        drawTime: 'afterDatasetsDraw',
                                        content: 'Lowest Offer:‚Çπ' + parseInt(Prices.Price.MinOfferPrice),
                                        enabled: true,
                                        position: "start",
                                        font: {
                                            size: 10
                                        },
                                        padding: 3,
                                        display: true
                                    }
                                });
                            }
                        } else {
                            if ("MinOfferPrice"in Prices.Price && Prices.Price.MinOfferPrice && Prices.Price.MinOfferPrice != null) {
                                ChartOptions.plugins.annotation.annotations.push({
                                    type: 'line',
                                    mode: 'horizontal',
                                    scaleID: 'y',
                                    value: Prices.Price.MinOfferPrice,
                                    borderColor: '#28a74599',
                                    borderWidth: 1,
                                    label: {
                                        backgroundColor: '#28a745bb',
                                        drawTime: 'afterDatasetsDraw',
                                        content: 'Lowest Offer:‚Çπ' + parseInt(Prices.Price.MinOfferPrice),
                                        enabled: true,
                                        position: "start",
                                        font: {
                                            size: 10
                                        },
                                        padding: 3,
                                        display: true
                                    }
                                });
                            }
                        }
                        if ("MaxPrice"in Prices.Price && Prices.Price.MaxPrice && Prices.Price.MaxPrice != null) {
                            ChartOptions.plugins.annotation.annotations.push({
                                type: 'line',
                                mode: 'horizontal',
                                scaleID: 'y',
                                value: Prices.Price.MaxPrice,
                                borderColor: '#ff534b99',
                                borderWidth: 1,
                                label: {
                                    backgroundColor: '#ff534bbb',
                                    drawTime: 'afterDatasetsDraw',
                                    content: 'Highest:‚Çπ' + Prices.Price.MaxPrice,
                                    enabled: true,
                                    position: "start",
                                    font: {
                                        size: 10
                                    },
                                    padding: 3,
                                    display: true
                                }
                            });
                        }
                    } else {
                        if ("MinPrice"in Prices.Price && Prices.Price.MinPrice && Prices.Price.MinPrice != null && "MinOfferPrice"in Prices.Price && Prices.Price.MinOfferPrice && Prices.Price.MinOfferPrice != null && Prices.Price.MinOfferPrice < Prices.Price.MinPrice) {
                            ChartOptions.plugins.annotation.annotations.push({
                                type: 'line',
                                mode: 'horizontal',
                                scaleID: 'y',
                                value: Prices.Price.MinOfferPrice,
                                borderColor: '#28a74599',
                                borderWidth: 1,
                                label: {
                                    backgroundColor: '#28a745bb',
                                    drawTime: 'afterDatasetsDraw',
                                    content: 'Lowest Offer:‚Çπ' + parseInt(Prices.Price.MinOfferPrice),
                                    enabled: true,
                                    position: "start",
                                    font: {
                                        size: 10
                                    },
                                    padding: 3,
                                    display: true
                                }
                            });
                        }
                    }
                    if ("TotalPrice"in Prices.Price && Prices.Price.TotalPrice && Prices.Price.TotalPrice != null) {
                        ChartOptions.plugins.annotation.annotations.push({
                            type: 'line',
                            mode: 'horizontal',
                            scaleID: 'y',
                            value: Prices.Price.TotalPrice / Prices.Price.Count,
                            borderColor: '#ffc10799',
                            borderWidth: 1,
                            label: {
                                backgroundColor: '#ffc107bb',
                                drawTime: 'afterDatasetsDraw',
                                content: 'Average:‚Çπ' + parseInt(Prices.Price.TotalPrice / Prices.Price.Count),
                                enabled: true,
                                position: "start",
                                font: {
                                    size: 10
                                },
                                padding: 3,
                                display: true
                            }
                        });
                    }
                    if ("Event"in Prices && Prices.Event != null && Array.isArray(Prices.Event) && Prices.Event.length > 0) {
                        for (let i = 0; i < Prices.Event.length; i++) {
                            ChartOptions.plugins.annotation.annotations.push({
                                type: 'box',
                                xMin: Prices.Event[i].Start,
                                xMax: Prices.Event[i].End,
                                backgroundColor: '#ffc10733',
                                borderWidth: 0,
                                label: {
                                    color: '#ff534b99',
                                    drawTime: 'afterDatasetsDraw',
                                    content: Prices.Event[i].Name,
                                    enabled: false,
                                    position: "center",
                                    font: {
                                        size: 10
                                    },
                                    rotation: 90,
                                    display: false
                                }
                            });
                        }
                    }
                    UpdateChartAnotations(PriceAnotationStarts, false);
                }
                ChartConfigs.options = ChartOptions;
                ChartConfigs.data.datasets = ChartDataSets;
                setTimeout( () => {
                    try {
                        chart = new Chart(canvas,ChartConfigs);
                        setTimeout( () => {
                            UpdateEnabled();
                            UpdateChartZoom("reset");
                            UpdateSelectedTimeStats();
                        }
                        , 1000);
                    } catch (error) {}
                }
                , 500)
            }
        }
    }
    ;function UpdateChartAnotations(Stats, isUpdate=true) {
        ChartOptions.plugins.annotation.annotations = ChartOptions.plugins.annotation.annotations.filter(function(element) {
            return element.type != "line"
        });
        if (Stats.Highest != null) {
            let TempData = parseInt(Stats.Highest + ((Stats.Lowest != null) ? ((Stats.Highest * 5 / 100) + (Stats.Lowest * 5 / 100)) / 2 : (Stats.Highest * 5 / 100)));
            if (TempData > 0) {
                ChartOptions.plugins.zoom.pan.rangeMax.y = TempData;
                ChartOptions.plugins.zoom.zoom.rangeMax.y = TempData;
                ChartOptions.plugins.zoom.limits.y.max = TempData;
                ChartOptions.scales.y.max = TempData;
            }
        }
        if (Stats.LowestOffer != null) {
            let TempData = null;
            if (Stats.Lowest != null && Stats.Lowest < Stats.LowestOffer) {
                TempData = parseInt(Stats.Lowest - ((Stats.Highest != null) ? ((Stats.Highest * 5 / 100) + (Stats.Lowest * 5 / 100)) / 2 : (Stats.Lowest * 5 / 100)));
            } else {
                TempData = parseInt(Stats.LowestOffer - ((Stats.Highest != null) ? ((Stats.Highest * 5 / 100) + (Stats.LowestOffer * 5 / 100)) / 2 : (Stats.LowestOffer * 5 / 100)));
            }
            TempData = (TempData < 0) ? 0 : TempData;
            if (TempData > 0) {
                ChartOptions.plugins.zoom.pan.rangeMin.y = TempData;
                ChartOptions.plugins.zoom.zoom.rangeMin.y = TempData;
                ChartOptions.plugins.zoom.limits.y.min = TempData;
                ChartOptions.scales.y.min = TempData;
            }
        } else if (Stats.Lowest != null) {
            let TempData = parseInt(Stats.Lowest - ((Stats.Highest != null) ? ((Stats.Highest * 5 / 100) + (Stats.Lowest * 5 / 100)) / 2 : (Stats.Lowest * 5 / 100)));
            TempData = (TempData < 0) ? 0 : TempData;
            if (TempData > 0) {
                ChartOptions.plugins.zoom.pan.rangeMin.y = TempData;
                ChartOptions.plugins.zoom.zoom.rangeMin.y = TempData;
                ChartOptions.plugins.zoom.limits.y.min = TempData;
                ChartOptions.scales.y.min = TempData;
            }
        }
        if (Stats.Highest != Stats.Lowest) {
            if (Stats.Highest != null) {
                if (Stats.Lowest != null) {
                    if (Stats.Highest > Stats.Lowest) {
                        DefaultAnotations.Highest.value = parseInt(Stats.Highest);
                        ChartOptions.plugins.annotation.annotations.push(DefaultAnotations.Highest);
                        DefaultAnotations.Lowest.value = parseInt(Stats.Lowest);
                        ChartOptions.plugins.annotation.annotations.push(DefaultAnotations.Lowest);
                    }
                } else {
                    DefaultAnotations.Highest.value = parseInt(Stats.Highest);
                    ChartOptions.plugins.annotation.annotations.push(DefaultAnotations.Highest);
                }
            } else {
                if (Stats.Lowest != null) {
                    DefaultAnotations.Lowest.value = parseInt(Stats.Lowest);
                    ChartOptions.plugins.annotation.annotations.push(DefaultAnotations.Lowest);
                }
            }
        }
        if (Stats.LowestOffer != null) {
            if (Stats.Lowest != null) {
                if (Stats.LowestOffer < Stats.Lowest) {
                    DefaultAnotations.LowestOffer.value = parseInt(Stats.LowestOffer);
                    ChartOptions.plugins.annotation.annotations.push(DefaultAnotations.LowestOffer);
                }
            } else {
                DefaultAnotations.LowestOffer.value = parseInt(Stats.LowestOffer);
                ChartOptions.plugins.annotation.annotations.push(DefaultAnotations.LowestOffer);
            }
        }
        if (Stats.Total != null && Stats.Count != null && Stats.Count > 0) {
            DefaultAnotations.Average.value = parseInt(Stats.Total / Stats.Count);
            ChartOptions.plugins.annotation.annotations.push(DefaultAnotations.Average);
        }
        if (isUpdate) {
            chart.update();
        }
    }
    function UpdateSelectedTimeStats() {
        let CurrentScalesMin = chart.options.scales.x.min;
        let CurrentScalesMax = chart.options.scales.x.max;
        let CurrentPriceDataset = chart.getDatasetMeta(chart.getVisibleDatasetCount() - 1).data;
        let CurrentOfferPriceDataset = [];
        let NewStatsData = {
            Highest: null,
            Lowest: null,
            Total: 0,
            Count: 0,
            LowestOffer: null,
            Date: {
                Start: CurrentScalesMin,
                End: CurrentScalesMax
            }
        };
        CurrentPriceDataset = CurrentPriceDataset.filter(function(element) {
            return element.$context.parsed.y != null && element.$context.parsed.x >= CurrentScalesMin && element.$context.parsed.x <= CurrentScalesMax
        });
        if (chart.getVisibleDatasetCount() > 1) {
            CurrentOfferPriceDataset = chart.getDatasetMeta(0).data;
            CurrentOfferPriceDataset = CurrentOfferPriceDataset.filter(function(element) {
                return element.$context.parsed.y != null && element.$context.parsed.x >= CurrentScalesMin && element.$context.parsed.x <= CurrentScalesMax
            });
            if (CurrentOfferPriceDataset.length > 0) {
                CurrentOfferPriceDataset.forEach(element => {
                    if (NewStatsData.LowestOffer == null) {
                        NewStatsData.LowestOffer = element.$context.raw.y;
                    } else if (NewStatsData.LowestOffer > element.$context.raw.y) {
                        NewStatsData.LowestOffer = element.$context.raw.y;
                    }
                }
                );
            }
        }
        CurrentPriceDataset.forEach(element => {
            if (NewStatsData.Highest == null) {
                NewStatsData.Highest = element.$context.raw.y;
            } else if (NewStatsData.Highest < element.$context.raw.y) {
                NewStatsData.Highest = element.$context.raw.y;
            }
            if (NewStatsData.Lowest == null) {
                NewStatsData.Lowest = element.$context.raw.y;
            } else if (NewStatsData.Lowest > element.$context.raw.y) {
                NewStatsData.Lowest = element.$context.raw.y;
            }
            NewStatsData.Count++;
            NewStatsData.Total += element.$context.raw.y;
        }
        );
        if (NewStatsData.Highest == null && NewStatsData.Lowest == null && NewStatsData.LowestOffer == null) {
            document.getElementsByClassName("chart-price-limit")[0].classList.add("d-none")
        } else {
            document.getElementsByClassName("chart-price-limit")[0].classList.remove("d-none")
        }
        if (NewStatsData.Highest == null) {
            document.getElementsByClassName("chart-price-highest")[0].getElementsByClassName("amount")[0].innerHTML = " - ";
        } else {
            document.getElementsByClassName("chart-price-highest")[0].getElementsByClassName("amount")[0].innerHTML = "‚Çπ" + parseInt(NewStatsData.Highest);
        }
        if (NewStatsData.Count == 0) {
            document.getElementsByClassName("chart-price-average")[0].getElementsByClassName("amount")[0].innerHTML = " - ";
        } else {
            document.getElementsByClassName("chart-price-average")[0].getElementsByClassName("amount")[0].innerHTML = "‚Çπ" + parseInt(NewStatsData.Total / NewStatsData.Count)
        }
        if (NewStatsData.Lowest == null) {
            document.getElementsByClassName("chart-price-lowest")[0].getElementsByClassName("amount")[0].innerHTML = " - ";
        } else {
            document.getElementsByClassName("chart-price-lowest")[0].getElementsByClassName("amount")[0].innerHTML = "‚Çπ" + parseInt(NewStatsData.Lowest);
        }
        if (NewStatsData.Lowest != null && NewStatsData.Count != 0 && NewStatsData.Highest != null) {
            let avg = NewStatsData.Total / NewStatsData.Count;
            let min = NewStatsData.Lowest;
            let max = NewStatsData.Highest;
            let percent = 50;
            if (max !== min) {
                percent = ((avg - min) / (max - min)) * 100;
                percent = Math.max(0, Math.min(100, percent));
            }
            document.getElementsByClassName("price-average")[0].style.marginLeft = percent + "%";
        }
        UpdateChartAnotations(NewStatsData);
    }
    function FetchPrices() {
        fetch("https://pricehistory.app/" + "api/price/" + "1FVhrpce", {
            method: "post",
            headers: FetchHeaders
        }).then( (response) => response.json()).then( (prices) => {
            setTimeout( () => {
                UpdatePrices(prices);
            }
            , 100)
        }
        ).catch( (err) => {
            console.log("Error", err, err.message);
            document.getElementById("PriceHistoryChart").style.display = "none !important";
        }
        )
    }
    ;function IsPricesChange() {
        fetch("https://pricehistory.app/" + "api/change/" + "1FVhrpce", {
            method: "post",
            headers: FetchHeaders
        }).then( (response) => response.json()).then( (response) => {
            document.querySelectorAll(".current-price-details").forEach(block => {
                block.classList.remove("current-price-details");
            }
            );
            if ("status"in response && response.status) {
                const priceChangeDiv = document.getElementById('price-change-div');
                const priceChangeRefresh = document.getElementById('price-change-refresh');
                const priceChangeCancel = document.getElementById('price-change-cancel');
                priceChangeDiv.getElementsByTagName("p")[0].innerHTML = "Prices has been changed. Please refresh the page.";
                priceChangeDiv.classList.remove("d-none");
                let countdownRefresh = 10;
                function refreshPage() {
                    location.reload();
                }
                function cancelRefreshTimer() {
                    clearInterval(timerRefresh);
                    priceChangeDiv.classList.add("d-none");
                }
                function updateCountdown() {
                    countdownRefresh--;
                    if (countdownRefresh === 0) {
                        refreshPage();
                    } else {
                        priceChangeRefresh.innerText = `Refresh(${countdownRefresh}s)`;
                    }
                }
                priceChangeRefresh.addEventListener('click', refreshPage);
                priceChangeCancel.addEventListener('click', cancelRefreshTimer);
                const timerRefresh = setInterval(updateCountdown, 1000);
            }
        }
        ).catch( (err) => {
            document.querySelectorAll(".current-price-details").forEach(block => {
                block.classList.remove("current-price-details");
            }
            );
            console.log("Error", err, err.message);
        }
        );
    }

    function DataDecrypt(data, key) {
        data = atob(data);
        let result = '';
        for (let i = 0; i < data.length; i++) {
            result += String.fromCharCode(data.charCodeAt(i) ^ key.charCodeAt(i % key.length));
        }
        return result;
    }
    let CachedKey = 'O7TXnQ9BzPhkqL3vANf2igREWoMFrjxZwaIYuHt4b5UJs068CcmDVKSdl1epyG';
    document.addEventListener("DOMContentLoaded", function(event) {
        try {
            UpdatePrices(JSON.parse(DataDecrypt(PagePriceHistoryDataSet, CachedKey)));
        } catch (error) {}
    });
    IsPricesChange();
    function refreshPrice() {
        let ResponseBlock = document.getElementById("refresh-price-response");
        fetch("https://pricehistory.app/" + "api/report/refresh/" + "1FVhrpce", {
            method: "post",
            headers: FetchHeaders,
            body: JSON.stringify({})
        }).then( (response) => response.json()).then( (response) => {
            ResponseBlock.innerHTML = "</span class=\"text-dark\"> Your request received. New Price will be updated Soon <span>";
            ResponseBlock.classList.remove("d-none");
        }
        ).catch( (err) => {
            ResponseBlock.classList.remove("d-none");
            console.log("Error", err, err.message);
            ResponseBlock.innerHTML = "</span class=\"text-dark\">Sorry,Something Went Wrong! <span>";
        }
        );
    }

<script>
    function SelectImageList(imgs) {
        var expandImg = document.getElementById("expandedImg");
        expandImg.src = imgs.src;
        expandImg.parentElement.style.display = "block";
    }
    function enterFullscreen() {
        body.classList.add('fullscreen');
    }
    function exitFullscreen() {
        body.classList.remove('fullscreen');
    }
    document.getElementById("chart-action-button-fullscreen-exit").addEventListener("click", function() {
        exitFullscreen();
    });
    document.getElementById("chart-action-button-fullscreen").addEventListener("click", function() {
        body.classList.toggle('fullscreen');
    });
    const body = document.body;
    document.addEventListener('keydown', (event) => {
        if (event.key === 'Escape' && body.classList.contains('fullscreen')) {
            exitFullscreen();
        }
    }
    );
    document.getElementById("chart-action-button-download").addEventListener("click", function() {
        saveCanvasAsImage();
    });
    document.getElementById("chart-action-button-copy").addEventListener("click", function() {
        const canvas = document.getElementById('PriceHistoryChart');
        canvas.toBlob(function(blob) {
            const item = new ClipboardItem({
                'image/png': blob
            });
            navigator.clipboard.write([item]).then(function() {
                console.log('Image copied to clipboard');
            }, function(error) {
                console.error('Failed to copy image:', error);
            });
        });
    });
    function saveCanvasAsImage() {
        const imageDataURL = document.getElementById('PriceHistoryChart').toDataURL('image/png');
        const link = document.createElement('a');
        link.href = imageDataURL;
        link.download = 'Price History of Samsung Galaxy A55 5G Awesome Iceblue 8GB.png';
        document.body.appendChild(link);
        link.click();
        document.body.removeChild(link);
    }
    function isElementInViewport(el) {
        if (!el)
            return false;
        const rect = el.getBoundingClientRect();
        return (rect.top < window.innerHeight && rect.bottom > 0 && rect.left < window.innerWidth && rect.right > 0);
    }
    function toggleBottomOverview() {
        const standingBtn = document.querySelector('.standing-buy-button');
        const bottomOverview = document.querySelector('.ph-bottom-overview');
        if (!standingBtn || !bottomOverview)
            return;
        if (isElementInViewport(standingBtn)) {
            bottomOverview.classList.add("d-none");
        } else {
            bottomOverview.classList.remove("d-none");
        }
    }
    window.addEventListener('scroll', toggleBottomOverview);
    window.addEventListener('resize', toggleBottomOverview);
    document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', toggleBottomOverview);
</script>

<script>
    document.querySelectorAll('.redirect-link').forEach(link => {
        link.addEventListener('click', function(e) {
            e.preventDefault();
            if (this.classList.contains("external-link")) {
                window.open(atob(this.getAttribute("data-link")), "_blank");
                InitiatecreatePopup();
                return;
            }
            window.open('https://pricehistory.app' + "/" + "redirect/" + this.getAttribute("data-link"), "_blank");
            InitiatecreatePopup();
        });
    }
    );
</script>

<script>
    function createPopup(Pid, titleText, subtitleText, buttonText, buttonLink) {
        const popup = document.createElement('div');
        popup.id = 'modern-popup';
        Object.assign(popup.style, {
            position: 'fixed',
            top: '50%',
            left: '50%',
            transform: 'translate(-50%,75%)',
            width: '350px',
            padding: '20px',
            backgroundColor: '#fff',
            boxShadow: '0 4px 8px rgba(0,0,0,0.2)',
            borderRadius: '10px',
            zIndex: '1000',
            textAlign: 'center',
            opacity: '0',
            transition: 'opacity 0.3s ease'
        });
        popup.innerHTML = ` <h2 style="margin:0 0 10px;font-size:18px;color:#333;">‚ú® ${titleText}‚ú®</h2> <p style="margin:0 0 15px;font-size:14px;color:#555;">${subtitleText}</p> <button id="popup-btn" style="padding:10px 20px;background:#007bff;color:#fff;border:none;border-radius:5px;cursor:pointer;">${buttonText}</button> <button id="popup-close" style="position:absolute;top:5px;right:10px;background:none;border:none;font-size:18px;cursor:pointer;">√ó</button> `;
        const backdrop = document.createElement('div');
        Object.assign(backdrop.style, {
            position: 'fixed',
            top: '0',
            left: '0',
            width: '100%',
            height: '100%',
            backgroundColor: 'rgba(0,0,0,0.5)',
            zIndex: '999',
        });
        document.body.appendChild(backdrop);
        document.body.style.overflow = 'hidden';
        document.body.appendChild(popup);
        document.getElementById('popup-btn').onclick = () => {
            window.open(buttonLink, '_blank');
            updatePopup({
                Id: Pid,
                Action: 'open'
            });
            popup.remove();
            backdrop.remove();
            document.body.style.overflow = '';
        }
        ;
        document.getElementById('popup-close').onclick = () => {
            updatePopup({
                Id: Pid,
                Action: 'close'
            });
            popup.remove();
            backdrop.remove();
            document.body.style.overflow = '';
        }
        ;
        backdrop.onclick = () => {
            updatePopup({
                Id: Pid,
                Action: 'close'
            });
            popup.remove();
            backdrop.remove();
            document.body.style.overflow = '';
        }
        ;
        setTimeout( () => popup.style.opacity = '1', 100);
    }
    function updatePopup(data) {
        try {
            let popupData = JSON.parse(localStorage.getItem("popupData")) || [];
            const existingPopupIndex = popupData.findIndex(p => p.Id === data.Id);
            if (existingPopupIndex !== -1) {
                popupData[existingPopupIndex].a = data.Action;
                popupData[existingPopupIndex].t = new Date().getTime();
            } else {
                popupData.push({
                    Id: data.Id,
                    a: data.Action,
                    t: new Date().getTime()
                });
            }
            localStorage.setItem("popupData", JSON.stringify(popupData));
        } catch (error) {
            console.error("Error updating popup data in localStorage:", error);
        }
    }
    function InitiatecreatePopup() {
        const Popups = [{
            Id: 4,
            Title: "üì± Price History App Mobile App",
            Subtitle: "Download our mobile app for the best experience and exclusive features.",
            ButtonText: "üì• Download Now",
            ButtonLink: "https://onelink.to/bds36n"
        }, {
            Id: 1,
            Title: "üí¨ Join us on WhatsApp",
            Subtitle: "Join our WhatsApp channel and never miss loot deals!",
            ButtonText: "üîó Join Channel Now",
            ButtonLink: "https://pricehistory.app/whatsapp"
        }, {
            Id: 5,
            Title: "üì¢ Join our Telegram Channel",
            Subtitle: "Get instant updates on the latest deals and offers.",
            ButtonText: "üîó Join Now",
            ButtonLink: "https://pricehistory.app/telegram"
        }, {
            Id: 7,
            Title: "üß© Install our Chrome Extension",
            Subtitle: "Get the best deals directly in your browser with our Chrome Extension.",
            ButtonText: "üîó Install Now",
            ButtonLink: "https://chromewebstore.google.com/detail/price-history-extension-p/agccifdcgciljchfofenkoboeehkmjkl?hl=en"
        }, {
            Id: 3,
            Title: "üê¶ Follow us on Twitter",
            Subtitle: "Stay updated with our latest news and offers.",
            ButtonText: "üîó Follow Now",
            ButtonLink: "https://x.com/pricehistory_"
        }, {
            Id: 6,
            Title: "üì∏ Follow us on Instagram",
            Subtitle: "Discover exclusive content and updates on our Instagram.",
            ButtonText: "üîó Follow Now",
            ButtonLink: "https://instagram.com/pricehistory_app"
        }];
        try {
            const popupData = JSON.parse(localStorage.getItem("popupData")) || [];
            const now = new Date().getTime();
            for (const popup of Popups) {
                const existingPopup = popupData.find(p => p.Id === popup.Id);
                if (!existingPopup) {
                    createPopup(popup.Id, popup.Title, popup.Subtitle, popup.ButtonText, popup.ButtonLink);
                    break;
                } else {
                    const timeDiff = now - existingPopup.t;
                    const sevenDays = 7 * 24 * 60 * 60 * 1000;
                    const oneMonth = 30 * 24 * 60 * 60 * 1000;
                    if ((existingPopup.a === 'close' && timeDiff > sevenDays) || (existingPopup.a === 'open' && timeDiff > oneMonth)) {
                        createPopup(popup.Id, popup.Title, popup.Subtitle, popup.ButtonText, popup.ButtonLink);
                        break;
                    }
                }
            }
        } catch (error) {
            console.error("Error processing popup logic:", error);
        }
    }
</script>
